Grammar

    0 $accept: nikola $end

    1 nikola: statements

    2 statements: statement statements
    3           | ε

    4 statement: expression ";"
    5          | assignment-statement

    6 assignment-statement: expression "=" expression ";"
    7                     | expression "<-" expression ";"
    8                     | expression "+=" expression ";"
    9                     | expression "-=" expression ";"
   10                     | expression "*=" expression ";"
   11                     | expression "/=" expression ";"
   12                     | expression "//=" expression ";"
   13                     | expression "^=" expression ";"
   14                     | expression "%=" expression ";"
   15                     | expression "+<=" expression ";"
   16                     | expression "-<=" expression ";"
   17                     | expression "*<=" expression ";"
   18                     | expression "/<=" expression ";"
   19                     | expression "//<=" expression ";"
   20                     | expression "^<=" expression ";"
   21                     | expression "%<=" expression ";"
   22                     | expression "&=" expression ";"
   23                     | expression "|=" expression ";"
   24                     | expression "^^=" expression ";"
   25                     | expression "~=" expression ";"
   26                     | expression "<<=" expression ";"
   27                     | expression ">>=" expression ";"
   28                     | expression "&<=" expression ";"
   29                     | expression "|<=" expression ";"
   30                     | expression "^^<=" expression ";"
   31                     | expression "~<=" expression ";"
   32                     | expression "<<<=" expression ";"
   33                     | expression ">><=" expression ";"

   34 expression: literal
   35           | name
   36           | "(" expression ")"
   37           | expression "+" expression
   38           | expression "-" expression
   39           | expression "*" expression
   40           | expression "/" expression
   41           | expression "//" expression
   42           | expression "%" expression
   43           | expression "^" expression
   44           | expression "+<" expression
   45           | expression "-<" expression
   46           | expression "*<" expression
   47           | expression "/<" expression
   48           | expression "//<" expression
   49           | expression "^<" expression
   50           | expression "%<" expression
   51           | expression "&&" expression
   52           | expression "||" expression
   53           | expression "<" expression
   54           | expression "<=" expression
   55           | expression "<=>" expression
   56           | expression ">=" expression
   57           | expression ">" expression
   58           | expression "==" expression
   59           | expression "!=" expression
   60           | "!" expression
   61           | expression "&" expression
   62           | expression "|" expression
   63           | expression "^^" expression
   64           | "~" expression
   65           | expression "<<" expression
   66           | expression ">>" expression
   67           | expression "&<" expression
   68           | expression "|<" expression
   69           | expression "^^<" expression
   70           | expression "~<" expression
   71           | expression "<<<" expression
   72           | expression ">><" expression
   73           | expression "." IDENTIFIER
   74           | "++" expression
   75           | "--" expression
   76           | expression "++"
   77           | expression "--"
   78           | "*" expression
   79           | "&" expression
   80           | "-" expression
   81           | expression "?" expression ":"
   82           | expression "is" expression
   83           | expression "in" expression
   84           | expression "..."
   85           | "typeof" "(" expression ")"
   86           | "sizeof" "(" expression ")"
   87           | "as" "<" name ">" "(" expression ")"
   88           | "static_assert" "(" expression ")"
   89           | "pure" "(" expression ")"
   90           | "nothrow" "(" expression ")"
   91           | "new" name "{" function_argument_list "}"
   92           | "new" "dynamic" name "{" function_argument_list "}"
   93           | name "(" function_argument_list ")"
   94           | "(" expression ")" "(" function_argument_list ")"
   95           | expression "." IDENTIFIER "(" function_argument_list ")"
   96           | array_index
   97           | array_index "(" function_argument_list ")"

   98 literal: INTEGER_LITERAL
   99        | REAL_LITERAL
  100        | COMPLEX_LITERAL
  101        | STRING_LITERAL
  102        | CHAR_LITERAL
  103        | "true"
  104        | "false"
  105        | "nptr"

  106 function_argument_list: function_argument_list0
  107                       | ε

  108 function_argument_list0: function_argument "," function_argument_list0
  109                        | function_argument

  110 function_argument: expression
  111                  | IDENTIFIER "=" expression

  112 array_index: name "[" array_slice_list "]"
  113            | expression "." IDENTIFIER "[" array_slice_list "]"
  114            | "(" expression ")" "[" array_slice_list "]"

  115 array_slice_list: array_slice "," array_slice_list
  116                 | array_slice

  117 array_slice: expression
  118            | expression ":"
  119            | ":" expression
  120            | expression ":" expression ":" expression
  121            | expression ":" expression ":"
  122            | ":" expression ":" expression

  123 name: IDENTIFIER
  124     | module_name

  125 module_name: IDENTIFIER "::" module_name
  126            | IDENTIFIER "::" IDENTIFIER
